{"type":"assistant","message":{"model":"claude-haiku-4-5-20251001","id":"msg_0152hFajMcD6c6wUJai6e6p1","type":"message","role":"assistant","content":[{"type":"tool_use","id":"toolu_01Efq6Qw3FDCVSzT2Yk12vvM","name":"Write","input":{"file_path":"/workspace/documentation.md","content":"# Apache Kafka KafkaConsumer API Reference Documentation\n\n## Table of Contents\n\n1. [Overview and Architecture](#overview-and-architecture)\n2. [Threading Model](#threading-model)\n3. [Core Types](#core-types)\n4. [Consumer Lifecycle](#consumer-lifecycle)\n5. [Subscription and Assignment](#subscription-and-assignment)\n6. [Polling and Data Fetching](#polling-and-data-fetching)\n7. [Offset Management](#offset-management)\n8. [Flow Control and Position Management](#flow-control-and-position-management)\n9. [Rebalancing and Consumer Groups](#rebalancing-and-consumer-groups)\n10. [Metadata and Monitoring](#metadata-and-monitoring)\n11. [Exception Handling](#exception-handling)\n12. [Configuration Properties](#configuration-properties)\n13. [Common Patterns and Best Practices](#common-patterns-and-best-practices)\n\n---\n\n## Overview and Architecture\n\n### Purpose\n\nThe `KafkaConsumer` is the primary client for consuming records from Apache Kafka topics. It provides:\n\n- **Scalability**: Multiple consumer instances in a group distribute partitions for parallel processing\n- **Fault tolerance**: Automatic failure detection with rebalancing and group coordination\n- **Flexibility**: Support for both automatic (group-managed) and manual partition assignment\n- **Offset management**: Track consumed positions with configurable commit strategies\n- **Flow control**: Pause/resume consumption at the partition level\n\n### Key Characteristics\n\n- **Single-threaded design**: A `KafkaConsumer` instance is not thread-safe except for the `wakeup()` method\n- **Event-driven**: All operations (including rebalancing) occur within `poll()` calls\n- **Group coordination**: Works with the Kafka broker for group membership and rebalancing\n- **TCP connections**: Maintains persistent connections to brokers; must be closed properly\n\n### Consumer Groups vs Manual Assignment\n\n**Consumer Groups** (dynamic assignment):\n- Multiple consumers with the same `group.id` coordinate to divide partitions\n- Automatic rebalancing when members join/leave\n- Use cases: horizontal scaling, fault tolerance\n- Enable via: `subscribe()` methods\n\n**Manual Assignment** (static assignment):\n- Consumer directly specifies partitions to consume\n- No group coordination or rebalancing\n- Use cases: single-machine consumption, external orchestration\n- Enable via: `assign()` method\n- Partitions never change without an explicit `assign()` call\n\n---\n\n## Threading Model\n\n### Thread Safety Constraints\n\nThe `KafkaConsumer` is **NOT thread-safe** for most operations:\n\n| Operation | Thread-Safe | Notes |\n|-----------|------------|-------|\n| `poll()` | ❌ No | Must be called from a single thread |\n| `subscribe()` | ❌ No | Must be called from consumer thread |\n| `assign()` | ❌ No | Must be called from consumer thread |\n| `commitSync()` | ❌ No | Must be called from consumer thread |\n| `commitAsync()` | ❌ No | Must be called from consumer thread |\n| `seek()` | ❌ No | Must be called from consumer thread |\n| `wakeup()` | ✅ YES | Safe to call from other threads |\n| `close()` | ❌ No | Should not be called during `poll()` |\n\n### Wakeup Mechanism\n\nThe `wakeup()` method is thread-safe and designed to interrupt a blocking `poll()` call:\n\n```java\n// From another thread:\nconsumer.wakeup();\n\n// In the consumer thread:\ntry {\n    while (true) {\n        ConsumerRecords<String, String> records = consumer.poll(Duration.ofMillis(100));\n        // process records\n    }\n} catch (WakeupException e) {\n    // Handle graceful shutdown\n}\n```\n\n### Multi-Threaded Processing Pattern\n\nFor processing records in parallel while maintaining correct offset management:\n\n```java\n// Consumer thread: polls and submits work\nExecutorService executor = Executors.newFixedThreadPool(4);\nMap<TopicPartition, Long> partitionOffsets = new HashMap<>();\n\ntry {\n    while (true) {\n        ConsumerRecords<String, String> records = consumer.poll(Duration.ofMillis(100));\n\n        for (TopicPartition tp : records.partitions()) {\n            List<ConsumerRecord<String, String>> partitionRecords = records.records(tp);\n\n            // Submit to executor\n            executor.submit(() -> {\n                for (ConsumerRecord<String, String> record : partitionRecords) {\n                    processRecord(record);\n                }\n            });\n\n            // Track offset for commit\n            ConsumerRecord<String, String> last = partitionRecords.get(partitionRecords.size() - 1);\n            partitionOffsets.put(tp, last.offset() + 1);\n        }\n\n        // Periodically commit processed offsets\n        if (!partitionOffsets.isEmpty()) {\n            Map<TopicPartition, OffsetAndMetadata> offsetsToCommit = new HashMap<>();\n            partitionOffsets.forEach((tp, offset) ->\n                offsetsToCommit.put(tp, new OffsetAndMetadata(offset)));\n\n            // Only commit after ALL workers have processed\n            consumer.pause(records.partitions());\n            executor.awaitTermination(5, TimeUnit.SECONDS);\n            consumer.commitSync(offsetsToCommit);\n            consumer.resume(records.partitions());\n        }\n    }\n} finally {\n    executor.shutdown();\n    consumer.close();\n}\n```\n\n---\n\n## Core Types\n\n### KafkaConsumer<K, V>\n\nThe main consumer class. Generic in key and value types.\n\n**Constructors:**\n\n```java\n// Config-based constructors\nKafkaConsumer(Properties properties)\nKafkaConsumer(Map<String, Object> configs)\n\n// With explicit deserializers\nKafkaConsumer(Properties properties,\n              Deserializer<K> keyDeserializer,\n              Deserializer<V> valueDeserializer)\nKafkaConsumer(Map<String, Object> configs,\n              Deserializer<K> keyDeserializer,\n              Deserializer<V> valueDeserializer)\n```\n\n### ConsumerRecords<K, V>\n\nContainer for records returned from a single `poll()` call.\n\n**Key Methods:**\n\n```java\n// Iteration\nIterator<ConsumerRecord<K, V>> iterator()\nIterable<ConsumerRecord<K, V>> records(TopicPartition partition)\nSet<TopicPartition> partitions()\n\n// Metadata\nint count()\nboolean isEmpty()\n\n// Position tracking\nMap<TopicPartition, Long> offset()  // Offsets of records in this batch\nMap<TopicPartition, OffsetAndMetadata> nextOffsets()  // Next offsets to commit\n\n// Timing\nlong timestamp()\n```\n\n**Behavioral Notes:**\n\n- Records are grouped by partition for efficient processing\n- `nextOffsets()` provides pre-calculated offsets for `commitSync()` calls\n- Records from a single `poll()` call are NOT guaranteed to come from all assigned partitions\n- Record order is preserved within each partition\n\n### ConsumerRecord<K, V>\n\nIndividual message fetched from Kafka.\n\n**Key Fields:**\n\n```java\nString topic()              // Topic name\nint partition()             // Partition number\nlong offset()               // Record offset within partition\nlong timestamp()            // Message timestamp\nTimestampType timestampType() // Type: CREATE_TIME or LOG_APPEND_TIME\nint serializedKeySize()     // Size in bytes\nint serializedValueSize()   // Size in bytes\nK key()                     // Deserialized key (or null)\nV value()                   // Deserialized value (or null)\nHeaders headers()           // Message headers\nOptional<Integer> leaderEpoch() // Leader epoch at time of write\n```\n\n### ConsumerRebalanceListener\n\nInterface for handling partition assignment changes.\n\n**Methods:**\n\n```java\ninterface ConsumerRebalanceListener {\n    // Called before losing partitions\n    void onPartitionsRevoked(Collection<TopicPartition> partitions)\n\n    // Called after gaining partitions\n    void onPartitionsAssigned(Collection<TopicPartition> partitions)\n\n    // Called when partitions are lost without notification (default calls revoked)\n    default void onPartitionsLost(Collection<TopicPartition> partitions) {\n        onPartitionsRevoked(partitions);\n    }\n}\n```\n\n**Callback Semantics:**\n\n- Called only within `poll()` calls\n- Revoke callbacks execute before assign callbacks\n- Exceptions propagate to the `poll()` call that triggered them\n- Callbacks serve as notifications only—exceptions don't prevent assignment\n- `WakeupException` can be raised from callbacks\n\n### OffsetAndMetadata\n\nRepresents a committed offset with optional metadata.\n\n```java\nclass OffsetAndMetadata {\n    // Constructors\n    OffsetAndMetadata(long offset)\n    OffsetAndMetadata(long offset, String metadata)\n    OffsetAndMetadata(long offset, Optional<Integer> leaderEpoch, String metadata)\n\n    // Accessors\n    long offset()\n    String metadata()\n    Optional<Integer> leaderEpoch()\n}\n```\n\n**Important Semantics:**\n\n- The offset represents the **next message to consume**, not the last consumed message\n- If last consumed message has offset 100, commit offset 101\n- Leader epoch helps detect log truncation issues\n- Metadata is application-specific (e.g., processing timestamp, hostname)\n\n### OffsetAndTimestamp\n\nResult of timestamp-based offset lookup.\n\n```java\nclass OffsetAndTimestamp {\n    long offset()              // Earliest offset >= target timestamp\n    long timestamp()           // Actual timestamp of message at offset\n}\n```\n\n---\n\n## Consumer Lifecycle\n\n### Initialization\n\n**Step 1: Create consumer**\n\n```java\nProperties props = new Properties();\nprops.put(\"bootstrap.servers\", \"localhost:9092\");\nprops.put(\"group.id\", \"my-group\");\nprops.put(\"key.deserializer\", StringDeserializer.class.getName());\nprops.put(\"value.deserializer\", StringDeserializer.class.getName());\n\nKafkaConsumer<String, String> consumer = new KafkaConsumer<>(props);\n```\n\n**Step 2: Subscribe or assign**\n\n```java\n// Dynamic assignment with consumer group\nconsumer.subscribe(Arrays.asList(\"topic1\", \"topic2\"));\n\n// OR manual assignment (mutually exclusive)\nconsumer.assign(Arrays.asList(\n    new TopicPartition(\"topic1\", 0),\n    new TopicPartition(\"topic1\", 1)\n));\n```\n\n**Step 3: Poll (group join happens here)**\n\n```java\n// First poll() triggers group join if subscribed\nConsumerRecords<String, String> records = consumer.poll(Duration.ofMillis(100));\n```\n\n### Joining a Consumer Group\n\nWhen a consumer first calls `poll()` after `subscribe()`:\n\n1. Consumer sends JoinGroup request with group ID\n2. Broker selects a group leader (first member to join)\n3. Leader runs partition assignment strategy (e.g., RangeAssignor)\n4. Members receive assignment via SyncGroup\n5. If custom listener provided, `onPartitionsAssigned()` is called\n6. Consumer begins fetching from assigned partitions\n\n**Timing Constraints:**\n\n- Group join must complete within `session.timeout.ms` (default 45 seconds)\n- If no `poll()` call for longer than `max.poll.interval.ms` (default 5 minutes), consumer is expelled\n- Expulsion is proactive—consumer will fail on next `commitSync()` with `CommitFailedException`\n\n### Graceful Shutdown\n\n```java\ntry {\n    while (true) {\n        ConsumerRecords<String, String> records = consumer.poll(Duration.ofMillis(100));\n        // process records\n    }\n} finally {\n    consumer.close()  // or consumer.close(Duration)\n}\n```\n\n**Close Behavior:**\n\n- Triggers `onPartitionsRevoked()` callback for all partitions\n- Sends LeaveGroup request to broker\n- Closes broker connections\n- Waits up to `default.api.timeout.ms` for graceful termination\n- Does NOT auto-commit offsets (unless explicitly configured)\n\n**Force Leave Option:**\n\n```java\nconsumer.close(new CloseOptions().timeout(Duration.ofSeconds(1)))\n```\n\n---\n\n## Subscription and Assignment\n\n### Dynamic Subscription (Consumer Groups)\n\n#### `subscribe(Collection<String> topics)`\n\nSubscribe to a fixed set of topics.\n\n```java\nconsumer.subscribe(Arrays.asList(\"topic1\", \"topic2\", \"topic3\"));\n```\n\n**Characteristics:**\n\n- Triggers rebalancing to distribute partitions\n- Responds dynamically to partition count changes\n- Incompatible with `assign()` (calling both raises exception)\n- New subscriptions override previous ones\n\n**Exceptions:**\n\n- `IllegalArgumentException`: if topics collection is empty or null\n- `ConcurrentModificationException`: if topics collection modified during call\n\n#### `subscribe(Collection<String> topics, ConsumerRebalanceListener listener)`\n\nSubscribe with rebalance callbacks.\n\n```java\nclass MyRebalanceListener implements ConsumerRebalanceListener {\n    public void onPartitionsRevoked(Collection<TopicPartition> partitions) {\n        // Commit offsets for revoked partitions\n        consumer.commitSync();\n    }\n\n    public void onPartitionsAssigned(Collection<TopicPartition> partitions) {\n        // Initialize state for new partitions\n        for (TopicPartition tp : partitions) {\n            long offset = loadOffsetFromDatabase(tp);\n            consumer.seek(tp, offset);\n        }\n    }\n}\n\nconsumer.subscribe(Arrays.asList(\"topic1\"), new MyRebalanceListener());\n```\n\n**Callback Timing:**\n\n- `onPartitionsRevoked()` called during rebalance, before new assignment\n- `onPartitionsAssigned()` called after rebalance completes, before polling resumes\n\n### Pattern-Based Subscription\n\n#### `subscribe(Pattern pattern)` and `subscribe(Pattern pattern, ConsumerRebalanceListener listener)`\n\nSubscribe to topics matching a regex pattern.\n\n```java\n// Subscribe to all topics starting with \"events-\"\nconsumer.subscribe(Pattern.compile(\"^events-.*\"), listener);\n```\n\n**Dynamic Topic Detection:**\n\n- Consumer periodically refreshes topic metadata\n- New topics matching pattern automatically assigned to members\n- Removed topics trigger rebalancing\n\n**Caveats:**\n\n- Pattern matching happens on all topics known to cluster\n- No way to un-subscribe from matched topics individually\n- Must unsubscribe and re-subscribe with different pattern\n\n### Manual Partition Assignment\n\n#### `assign(Collection<TopicPartition> partitions)`\n\nManually assign specific partitions.\n\n```java\nList<TopicPartition> partitions = Arrays.asList(\n    new TopicPartition(\"topic1\", 0),\n    new TopicPartition(\"topic1\", 1)\n);\nconsumer.assign(partitions);\n```\n\n**Characteristics:**\n\n- Disables consumer group coordination\n- No rebalancing occurs\n- No `onPartitionsAssigned()` callback\n- Partitions remain assigned until next `assign()` call\n- Can be called multiple times to change assignment\n\n**Behavior with Offsets:**\n\n- Consumer must explicitly seek to desired offset\n- No committed offset is used for position initialization\n- `commitSync()` still works but offsets stored only for bookkeeping\n\n### Subscription State Management\n\n#### `subscription()` - Get current subscription\n\n```java\nSet<String> topics = consumer.subscription();  // Returns empty set if assigned\n```\n\n#### `assignment()` - Get current assignment\n\n```java\nSet<TopicPartition> partitions = consumer.assignment();\n```\n\n#### `unsubscribe()`\n\nClear all subscriptions and assignments.\n\n```java\nconsumer.unsubscribe();  // Triggers onPartitionsRevoked() for all partitions\n```\n\n---\n\n## Polling and Data Fetching\n\n### The Poll Loop\n\n#### `poll(Duration timeout)`\n\nThe central method in Kafka consumer usage.\n\n```java\nConsumerRecords<String, String> records = consumer.poll(Duration.ofMillis(100));\n\nfor (ConsumerRecord<String, String> record : records) {\n    System.out.println(record.key() + \" -> \" + record.value());\n}\n```\n\n**Behavioral Semantics:**\n\nThe `poll()` method is complex and performs multiple functions:\n\n1. **Sends heartbeats** to maintain group membership (if subscribed)\n2. **Executes rebalance callbacks** if a rebalance was triggered\n3. **Fetches records** from brokers\n4. **Advances position** for successfully fetched records\n5. **Returns records** to the caller\n\n**Blocking Behavior:**\n\n- `timeout` parameter specifies maximum time to wait for records\n- During normal operation: returns quickly if records available, waits up to `timeout` if empty\n- During rebalance: `timeout` is exceeded while rebalance completes\n- Poll **may block longer than timeout** if rebalance callbacks take time\n- Timeout can be overridden by internal timers (e.g., metadata refresh)\n\n**Important Constraints:**\n\n- Must be called frequently to maintain group membership (at least once per `max.poll.interval.ms`)\n- Calling poll while processing prior batch can cause group expulsion\n- Only one `poll()` call can be in progress at a time (not thread-safe)\n\n**Return Value:**\n\n- `ConsumerRecords` object containing all fetched records\n- May be empty if no new records available\n- Records grouped by partition for efficient batch processing\n- Records are in order within each partition\n\n### Record Fetching\n\n#### Record Availability\n\nA record is available to the consumer when:\n\n1. It has been written to the partition\n2. All in-sync replicas have acknowledged it (for durability)\n3. If using `isolation.level=read_committed`: the transaction containing it is committed\n4. Position is <= record's offset\n\n#### Max Fetch Size\n\n`max.poll.records` configuration controls batch size:\n\n```properties\nmax.poll.records=500  # Default: fetch at most 500 records per poll\n```\n\nTrade-offs:\n- Lower values: more frequent polls, better responsiveness, higher overhead\n- Higher values: fewer polls, better throughput, more memory usage, longer processing deadlines\n\n#### Fetch Offset Management\n\nThe consumer tracks position per partition:\n\n```\nCommitted Offset     Position      End Offset\n      10      <---------11-------->      20\n\nConsumer will fetch from offset 11\nIf position >= end offset, no records available\n```\n\n---\n\n## Offset Management\n\n### Offset Concepts\n\n#### Position\n\nThe offset of the **next record** to be fetched.\n\n```java\nlong offset = consumer.position(partition);\n// If last fetched record was offset 100, position is 101\n```\n\n**Characteristics:**\n\n- Automatically advances when records are fetched via `poll()`\n- Can be manually set with `seek()`\n- Not persisted; resets after consumer restart\n\n#### Committed Offset\n\nThe last offset successfully committed to Kafka.\n\n```java\nMap<TopicPartition, OffsetAndMetadata> committed = consumer.committed(\n    Collections.singleton(partition)\n);\nOffsetAndMetadata oam = committed.get(partition);\nlong offset = oam.offset();  // 0 if never committed\n```\n\n**Characteristics:**\n\n- Persisted in `__consumer_offsets` topic\n- Used to resume after consumer restart\n- Can be committed via `commitSync()` or `commitAsync()`\n- Can be auto-committed based on time interval\n\n#### Offset Semantics\n\n**Critical Rule: Committed offset = next offset to read**\n\n```java\n// WRONG:\nConsumerRecord record = getLastRecord();\nconsumer.commitSync(record.offset());  // Commits record itself\n\n// RIGHT:\nConsumerRecord record = getLastRecord();\nconsumer.commitSync(record.offset() + 1);  // Commits offset of NEXT record\n\n// Or:\nconsumer.commitSync(Collections.singletonMap(partition,\n    new OffsetAndMetadata(record.offset() + 1)));\n```\n\n### Automatic Offset Committing\n\nWhen enabled, offsets are committed periodically:\n\n```properties\nenable.auto.commit=true              # Enable auto-commit\nauto.commit.interval.ms=5000         # Commit every 5 seconds\n```\n\n**Behavior:**\n\n- Commits all offsets from most recent `poll()` call\n- Offset committed = last fetched offset + 1\n- Happens asynchronously before next `poll()` call\n- No exception if commit fails (logged but not raised)\n\n**Risks:**\n\n- Records lost if consumer crashes between fetch and commit\n- At-least-once semantics: records may be re-delivered on restart\n- Cannot distinguish between processed and unprocessed records\n\n**Recommendation:** Disable for exactly-once semantics\n\n### Manual Offset Committing\n\n#### Synchronous Commit: `commitSync()`\n\n```java\ntry {\n    consumer.commitSync();  // Commits all offsets from last poll()\n} catch (CommitFailedException e) {\n    // Consumer no longer part of group, cannot commit\n    logger.error(\"Commit failed\", e);\n}\n```\n\n**Behavior:**\n\n- Blocks until commit succeeds or fails\n- Uses timeout from `default.api.timeout.ms`\n- Commits offsets for all fetched records from last `poll()` call\n- Fails immediately if `max.poll.interval.ms` exceeded (proactive expulsion)\n\n**Common Exception:**\n\n```\nCommitFailedException: The consumer is not part of an active consumer group\n```\n\nCauses:\n- Consumer not yet subscribed/joined group\n- Exceeded `max.poll.interval.ms` without calling `poll()`\n- Another consumer in group claims ownership of partition\n- Consumer was explicitly removed from group\n\n#### Synchronous Commit with Timeout: `commitSync(Duration timeout)`\n\n```java\nconsumer.commitSync(Duration.ofSeconds(5));  // Custom timeout\n```\n\n#### Explicit Offset Commit: `commitSync(Map<TopicPartition, OffsetAndMetadata> offsets)`\n\nCommit specific offsets (e.g., after processing only some records).\n\n```java\nMap<TopicPartition, OffsetAndMetadata> offsets = new HashMap<>();\nfor (TopicPartition tp : records.partitions()) {\n    List<ConsumerRecord<String, String>> partitionRecords = records.records(tp);\n\n    // Find last successfully processed record\n    ConsumerRecord<String, String> lastProcessed = findLastSuccessful(partitionRecords);\n\n    if (lastProcessed != null) {\n        offsets.put(tp, new OffsetAndMetadata(\n            lastProcessed.offset() + 1,\n            Optional.of(lastProcessed.leaderEpoch().orElse(-1)),\n            \"processed\"\n        ));\n    }\n}\n\nconsumer.commitSync(offsets);  // Commit only processed offsets\n```\n\n#### Asynchronous Commit: `commitAsync()`\n\n```java\nconsumer.commitAsync((offsets, exception) -> {\n    if (exception != null) {\n        logger.error(\"Commit failed for offsets: {}\", offsets, exception);\n        // Retry or store for later commit\n    } else {\n        logger.info(\"Commit succeeded\");\n    }\n});\n\n// Continue polling immediately, callback invoked later\nConsumerRecords<String, String> records = consumer.poll(Duration.ofMillis(100));\n```\n\n**Characteristics:**\n\n- Returns immediately without waiting\n- Callback invoked when commit result available\n- Multiple pending async commits: callbacks invoke in order\n- Failures typically retried automatically\n\n#### Asynchronous Commit with Callback: `commitAsync(Map<TopicPartition, OffsetAndMetadata> offsets, OffsetCommitCallback callback)`\n\n```java\nOffsetCommitCallback callback = (offsets, exception) -> {\n    if (exception != null) {\n        logger.error(\"Async commit failed\", exception);\n    }\n};\n\nconsumer.commitAsync(Collections.singletonMap(\n    partition,\n    new OffsetAndMetadata(nextOffset)\n), callback);\n```\n\n### Offset Commit Failures\n\n#### Retryable Failures\n\nThe consumer automatically retries:\n- Temporary network failures\n- Broker temporarily unavailable\n- Broker leadership changes during commit\n\n#### Non-Retryable Failures\n\nThe consumer does NOT retry:\n- `CommitFailedException`: consumer expelled from group\n- `AuthorizationException`: no permission to commit\n- Offset metadata too large (> 1MB)\n\n### Offset Reset Strategies\n\nIf position cannot be determined (no committed offset, consumer reset):\n\n```properties\nauto.offset.reset=earliest    # Start from beginning\nauto.offset.reset=latest      # Start from end\nauto.offset.reset=none        # Raise NoOffsetForPartitionException\n```\n\n**Applicable When:**\n\n- Consumer first joins group (no prior committed offset)\n- Partition added after consumer started\n- Consumer explicitly calls `seekToBeginning()` or `seekToEnd()`\n\n---\n\n## Flow Control and Position Management\n\n### Pause and Resume\n\n#### `pause(Collection<TopicPartition> partitions)`\n\nStop fetching from specified partitions.\n\n```java\n// Pause high-latency partition\nconsumer.pause(Collections.singleton(slowPartition));\n\n// Continue polling for other partitions\nConsumerRecords<String, String> records = consumer.poll(Duration.ofMillis(100));\n// slowPartition not included even if assigned\n```\n\n**Use Cases:**\n\n1. **Backpressure**: Downstream system is slow\n2. **Priority partitions**: Focus on high-priority topics first\n3. **Load balancing**: Redirect processing capacity\n4. **Throttling**: Rate-limit consumption\n\n**Important Notes:**\n\n- Paused partitions still count as \"assigned\"\n- Partition state does NOT persist through rebalance\n- `pause()` called during rebalance callback affects new assignment\n- Multiple `pause()` calls are cumulative\n\n#### `resume(Collection<TopicPartition> partitions)`\n\nResume fetching from paused partitions.\n\n```java\nconsumer.resume(Collections.singleton(slowPartition));\n```\n\n#### `paused()`\n\nGet the set of currently paused partitions.\n\n```java\nSet<TopicPartition> paused = consumer.paused();\n```\n\n### Position Control\n\n#### `seek(TopicPartition partition, long offset)`\n\nSet the offset to fetch on next `poll()`.\n\n```java\n// Seek to specific offset\nconsumer.seek(partition, 12345);\n\n// Next poll() starts from offset 12345\nConsumerRecords<String, String> records = consumer.poll(Duration.ofMillis(100));\n// First record will be offset 12345 (or next available)\n```\n\n**Semantics:**\n\n- Position is set immediately\n- Fetching starts at this offset on next `poll()`\n- Offset must be non-negative\n- Partition must be assigned to consumer\n\n**Exceptions:**\n\n- `IllegalArgumentException`: offset < 0\n- `IllegalStateException`: partition not assigned\n\n#### `seek(TopicPartition partition, OffsetAndMetadata offsetAndMetadata)`\n\nSeek with leader epoch information (for truncation detection).\n\n```java\nOffsetAndMetadata offsetWithEpoch = new OffsetAndMetadata(\n    12345,\n    Optional.of(leaderEpoch),  // Include leader epoch\n    \"\"\n);\nconsumer.seek(partition, offsetWithEpoch);\n```\n\n#### `position(TopicPartition partition)`\n\nGet the current position (next offset to fetch).\n\n```java\nlong nextOffset = consumer.position(partition);\n```\n\n**Behavior:**\n\n- Performs remote call if position not yet initialized\n- Blocks up to `default.api.timeout.ms`\n- Returns offset of next record to be fetched\n\n#### `position(TopicPartition partition, Duration timeout)`\n\nPosition with custom timeout.\n\n```java\nlong pos = consumer.position(partition, Duration.ofSeconds(10));\n```\n\n### Seeking to Beginning and End\n\n#### `seekToBeginning(Collection<TopicPartition> partitions)`\n\nSeek to the first available offset.\n\n```java\nconsumer.seekToBeginning(Collections.singleton(partition));\n// or all assigned partitions\nconsumer.seekToBeginning(Collections.emptyList());\n```\n\n**Behavior:**\n\n- Lazy evaluation: actual seek happens at next `poll()` call\n- Sets position to earliest offset in partition\n- Use `beginningOffsets()` to query without seeking\n\n#### `seekToEnd(Collection<TopicPartition> partitions)`\n\nSeek to the last offset.\n\n```java\nconsumer.seekToEnd(Collections.singleton(partition));\n```\n\n**Behavior:**\n\n- Lazy evaluation: actual seek happens at next `poll()` call\n- Sets position just past last message\n- If `isolation.level=read_committed`: seeks to Last Stable Offset (LSO)\n- Next `poll()` returns no records for this partition (unless new messages arrive)\n\n### Timestamp-Based Seeking\n\n#### `offsetsForTimes(Map<TopicPartition, Long> timestampsToSearch)`\n\nFind offsets for specific timestamps.\n\n```java\n// Find offset for records >= 1 hour ago\nlong oneHourAgo = System.currentTimeMillis() - 3600_000;\nMap<TopicPartition, Long> timestampMap = Collections.singletonMap(\n    partition,\n    oneHourAgo\n);\n\nMap<TopicPartition, OffsetAndTimestamp> result = consumer.offsetsForTimes(timestampMap);\n\nOffsetAndTimestamp oat = result.get(partition);\nif (oat != null) {\n    consumer.seek(partition, oat.offset());\n}\n```\n\n**Behavior:**\n\n- Returns earliest offset whose timestamp >= requested timestamp\n- Returns `null` if no matching offset found\n- Requires topic configured with `message.format.version >= 0.10`\n- Blocking call up to `default.api.timeout.ms`\n\n**Timestamps:**\n\n- Created by producer: `CreateTime` (default)\n- Added by broker: `LogAppendTime` (if configured)\n- Broker can have log compaction without timestamps\n\n### Beginning and End Offset Queries\n\n#### `beginningOffsets(Collection<TopicPartition> partitions)`\n\nQuery first available offset (doesn't seek).\n\n```java\nMap<TopicPartition, Long> beginnings = consumer.beginningOffsets(\n    Collections.singleton(partition)\n);\nlong firstOffset = beginnings.get(partition);\n```\n\n#### `endOffsets(Collection<TopicPartition> partitions)`\n\nQuery offset after last message (doesn't seek).\n\n```java\nMap<TopicPartition, Long> ends = consumer.endOffsets(\n    Collections.singleton(partition)\n);\nlong nextOffset = ends.get(partition);  // Offset to append next message\n```\n\n**Difference from seekToEnd:**\n- These methods only query; don't change position\n- Can be called even if partition not assigned\n- Useful for monitoring lag or validating offsets\n\n### Current Lag Calculation\n\n#### `currentLag(TopicPartition topicPartition)`\n\nGet approximate consumer lag.\n\n```java\nOptionalLong lag = consumer.currentLag(partition);\nif (lag.isPresent()) {\n    System.out.println(\"Lag: \" + lag.getAsLong() + \" records\");\n}\n```\n\n**Behavior:**\n\n- Returns `OptionalLong.empty()` if lag cannot be determined\n- Lag = `endOffset - position`\n- Based on cached metadata; may be approximate\n\n---\n\n## Rebalancing and Consumer Groups\n\n### Rebalance Triggers\n\nA rebalance occurs when:\n\n1. **New consumer joins group** (first `poll()` after subscribe)\n2. **Consumer leaves group** (`close()`, `unsubscribe()`, session timeout)\n3. **Partition count changes** (in subscribed topics)\n4. **Topic added** (if using regex subscription)\n5. **Consumer explicitly requests** (`enforceRebalance()`)\n\n### Rebalance Protocol\n\n**Classic (Eager) Rebalancing:**\n\n1. Stop: All consumers stop fetching\n2. Revoke: All consumers lose all partitions (even unchanged ones)\n3. Rebalance: Broker runs assignment strategy\n4. Assign: Consumers receive new assignment\n5. Resume: Consumers begin fetching\n\n**Cooperative Rebalancing:**\n\n1. Revoke: Consumers revoke only partitions they're losing\n2. Rebalance: Broker runs assignment strategy\n3. Assign: Consumers receive only new partitions\n4. Resume: Seamless transition with minimal stop\n\n### Consumer Rebalance Listener\n\n#### Implementing the Interface\n\n```java\npublic class MyRebalanceListener implements ConsumerRebalanceListener {\n    private final KafkaConsumer<?, ?> consumer;\n    private final Database database;\n\n    public MyRebalanceListener(KafkaConsumer<?, ?> consumer, Database database) {\n        this.consumer = consumer;\n        this.database = database;\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public void onPartitionsRevoked(Collection<TopicPartition> partitions) {\n        // CRITICAL: Commit offsets before losing partitions\n        try {\n            consumer.commitSync();\n        } catch (CommitFailedException e) {\n            logger.error(\"Failed to commit\", e);\n        }\n\n        // Clean up partition-local state\n        for (TopicPartition tp : partitions) {\n            flushPartitionCache(tp);\n        }\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public void onPartitionsAssigned(Collection<TopicPartition> partitions) {\n        // Initialize state for new partitions\n        for (TopicPartition tp : partitions) {\n            long offset = database.getOffset(tp);\n            if (offset >= 0) {\n                consumer.seek(tp, offset);\n            }\n        }\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public void onPartitionsLost(Collection<TopicPartition> partitions) {\n        // Partitions already reassigned; don't commit\n        logger.warn(\"Partitions lost without revoke callback: {}\", partitions);\n    }\n}\n\n// Register listener\nconsumer.subscribe(Arrays.asList(\"topic1\", \"topic2\"),\n    new MyRebalanceListener(consumer, database));\n```\n\n#### Callback Execution Context\n\n**When Called:**\n\n- Only within `poll()` calls\n- Before other operations resume\n- Synchronously (callback must return before `poll()` returns)\n\n**Exception Handling:**\n\n- Exceptions from callbacks propagate to the `poll()` call\n- Consumer is still notified of assignment (callback failure doesn't prevent assignment)\n- `WakeupException` can be raised from nested consumer calls\n\n**Callback Constraints:**\n\n- Cannot call `poll()` recursively\n- Can call `commitSync()`, `seek()`, `position()`, etc.\n- Cannot call `subscribe()`, `assign()`, `unsubscribe()`, `close()`\n\n### Proactive Consumer Expulsion\n\nIf consumer doesn't call `poll()` within `max.poll.interval.ms`:\n\n1. Consumer is expelled from group\n2. Partitions reassigned to other members\n3. Next `commitSync()` call raises `CommitFailedException`\n\n```properties\nmax.poll.interval.ms=300000  # 5 minutes default\n```\n\n**Recovery:**\n\n```java\ntry {\n    consumer.commitSync();\n} catch (CommitFailedException e) {\n    // Rejoin group by calling poll()\n    consumer.poll(Duration.ZERO);\n    // Then retry commit\n    consumer.commitSync();\n}\n```\n\n### Enforcing Rebalance\n\n#### `enforceRebalance()` and `enforceRebalance(String reason)`\n\nTrigger rebalance on next `poll()` call.\n\n```java\nconsumer.enforceRebalance(\"Rebalancing due to external event\");\n\n// Rebalance happens on next poll()\nconsumer.poll(Duration.ofMillis(100));  // Triggers rebalance\n```\n\n**Use Cases:**\n\n- External coordination signals need rebalancing\n- Graceful shutdown preparation\n- Handling partition assignment changes\n\n---\n\n## Metadata and Monitoring\n\n### Consumer Metadata\n\n#### `groupMetadata()`\n\nGet current group membership information.\n\n```java\nConsumerGroupMetadata metadata = consumer.groupMetadata();\n\nString groupId = metadata.groupId();        // Consumer group ID\nint generation = metadata.generationId();   // Generation ID (increments on rebalance)\nString memberId = metadata.memberId();      // Member ID assigned by broker\nOptional<String> groupInstanceId = metadata.groupInstanceId();  // Static assignment ID\n```\n\n**Use Cases:**\n\n- Pass to producer for transactional writes\n- Track generation for rebalance detection\n- Identify static group members\n\n#### `clientInstanceId(Duration timeout)`\n\nGet unique instance ID.\n\n```java\nUuid instanceId = consumer.clientInstanceId(Duration.ofSeconds(5));\n```\n\n### Partition Information\n\n#### `partitionsFor(String topic)` and `partitionsFor(String topic, Duration timeout)`\n\nList partitions for a topic.\n\n```java\nList<PartitionInfo> partitions = consumer.partitionsFor(\"topic1\");\n\nfor (PartitionInfo info : partitions) {\n    System.out.println(\"Partition: \" + info.partition());\n    System.out.println(\"  Leader: \" + info.leader());\n    System.out.println(\"  Replicas: \" + Arrays.toString(info.replicas()));\n    System.out.println(\"  In-Sync Replicas: \" + Arrays.toString(info.inSyncReplicas()));\n}\n```\n\n**Behavior:**\n\n- Performs remote call if topic metadata not cached\n- Blocks up to timeout\n- Returns null for unknown topics\n\n#### `listTopics()` and `listTopics(Duration timeout)`\n\nList all topics in cluster.\n\n```java\nMap<String, List<PartitionInfo>> allTopics = consumer.listTopics();\n\nfor (Map.Entry<String, List<PartitionInfo>> entry : allTopics.entrySet()) {\n    System.out.println(\"Topic: \" + entry.getKey());\n    System.out.println(\"  Partitions: \" + entry.getValue().size());\n}\n```\n\n### Metrics\n\n#### `metrics()`\n\nGet consumer metrics (network I/O, latencies, etc.).\n\n```java\nMap<MetricName, ? extends Metric> metrics = consumer.metrics();\n\nfor (Map.Entry<MetricName, ? extends Metric> entry : metrics.entrySet()) {\n    MetricName name = entry.getKey();\n    Metric metric = entry.getValue();\n\n    System.out.println(name.name() + \": \" + metric.value());\n}\n```\n\n**Common Metrics:**\n\n- `fetch-latency-avg`, `fetch-latency-max`: Fetch request latency\n- `records-consumed-total`: Total records fetched\n- `bytes-consumed-total`: Total bytes fetched\n- `commit-latency-avg`: Offset commit latency\n\n---\n\n## Exception Handling\n\n### Consumer Exceptions\n\n#### CommitFailedException\n\n```java\ntry {\n    consumer.commitSync();\n} catch (CommitFailedException e) {\n    // Consumer no longer owns partitions\n    logger.error(\"Cannot commit: not in group or partitions revoked\");\n}\n```\n\n**Causes:**\n\n- Consumer expelled from group (max.poll.interval.ms exceeded)\n- Partition reassigned to another consumer\n- Consumer not subscribed to any topics\n- Committing to unassigned partition\n\n**Recovery:**\n\n```java\ntry {\n    consumer.commitSync();\n} catch (CommitFailedException e) {\n    // Rejoin group\n    consumer.poll(Duration.ZERO);\n\n    // Retry commit\n    try {\n        consumer.commitSync();\n    } catch (CommitFailedException e2) {\n        logger.error(\"Still cannot commit after rejoin\");\n    }\n}\n```\n\n#### RebalanceInProgressException\n\n```java\ntry {\n    consumer.commitSync();\n} catch (RebalanceInProgressException e) {\n    // Rebalance in progress, try poll() first\n    consumer.poll(Duration.ZERO);\n    consumer.commitSync();  // Retry\n}\n```\n\n**When Raised:**\n\n- Calling `commitSync()` during rebalance (though callbacks usually prevent this)\n- Rebalance started but not yet complete\n\n#### WakeupException\n\n```java\ntry {\n    while (true) {\n        consumer.poll(Duration.ofMillis(100));\n    }\n} catch (WakeupException e) {\n    logger.info(\"Consumer awakened, shutting down\");\n    consumer.close();\n}\n```\n\n**Characteristics:**\n\n- Non-fatal: signals consumer should stop\n- Raised in `poll()` or other blocking calls\n- Thread-safe `wakeup()` method from another thread triggers it\n- Does NOT close consumer automatically\n\n#### InterruptException\n\n```java\ntry {\n    consumer.poll(Duration.ofMillis(100));\n} catch (InterruptException e) {\n    Thread.currentThread().interrupt();\n    logger.info(\"Consumer thread interrupted\");\n}\n```\n\n**When Raised:**\n\n- Consumer thread interrupted while blocked in API call\n- Similar to `WakeupException` but from thread interruption\n\n#### OffsetOutOfRangeException\n\n```java\ntry {\n    consumer.poll(Duration.ofMillis(100));\n} catch (OffsetOutOfRangeException e) {\n    logger.error(\"Offset out of range, seeking to beginning\");\n    consumer.seekToBeginning(e.partitions());\n    consumer.poll(Duration.ZERO);\n}\n```\n\n**When Raised:**\n\n- Position is beyond end of partition\n- Position is before beginning (deleted due to retention)\n- Offset reset strategy is `none`\n\n#### NoOffsetForPartitionException\n\n```java\ntry {\n    consumer.poll(Duration.ofMillis(100));\n} catch (NoOffsetForPartitionException e) {\n    logger.error(\"No offset for partition, using default strategy\");\n    // auto.offset.reset applies\n    consumer.poll(Duration.ZERO);\n}\n```\n\n**When Raised:**\n\n- No committed offset for partition\n- Partition new to consumer\n- Offset reset strategy is `none`\n\n#### InvalidOffsetException\n\n```java\ntry {\n    long pos = consumer.position(partition);\n} catch (InvalidOffsetException e) {\n    logger.error(\"Invalid position, resetting\");\n    consumer.seekToBeginning(Collections.singleton(partition));\n}\n```\n\n**When Raised:**\n\n- Current position cannot be determined\n- Requested offset is invalid\n- Log compaction has removed all committed offset data\n\n#### TimeoutException\n\n```java\ntry {\n    consumer.commitSync(Duration.ofSeconds(5));\n} catch (TimeoutException e) {\n    logger.error(\"Commit timeout, will retry asynchronously\");\n    consumer.commitAsync();\n}\n```\n\n**When Raised:**\n\n- API call timeout exceeded\n- Broker unavailable for entire duration\n- No response received from broker\n\n#### AuthenticationException and AuthorizationException\n\n```java\ntry {\n    consumer.poll(Duration.ofMillis(100));\n} catch (AuthenticationException e) {\n    logger.error(\"Authentication failed: {}\", e.getMessage());\n    // Check credentials and restart\n} catch (AuthorizationException e) {\n    logger.error(\"Not authorized to access topic: {}\", e.getMessage());\n    // Check ACLs\n}\n```\n\n#### FencedInstanceIdException\n\n```java\ntry {\n    consumer.poll(Duration.ofMillis(100));\n} catch (FencedInstanceIdException e) {\n    logger.error(\"Consumer instance fenced by broker\");\n    consumer.close();\n    // Create new consumer with same group.instance.id to rejoin\n}\n```\n\n**When Raised:**\n\n- Using static group membership with `group.instance.id`\n- Another instance with same ID joined group\n- Original instance should shut down\n\n### Exception Recovery Patterns\n\n#### Graceful Degradation\n\n```java\nlong retries = 0;\nlong maxRetries = 3;\n\nwhile (retries < maxRetries) {\n    try {\n        consumer.poll(Duration.ofMillis(100));\n        retries = 0;  // Reset on success\n    } catch (RetriableException e) {\n        retries++;\n        if (retries >= maxRetries) {\n            logger.error(\"Max retries exceeded\");\n            throw e;\n        }\n        Thread.sleep(1000 * retries);  // Exponential backoff\n    }\n}\n```\n\n#### Partition-Level Recovery\n\n```java\ntry {\n    ConsumerRecords<String, String> records = consumer.poll(Duration.ofMillis(100));\n\n    for (TopicPartition tp : records.partitions()) {\n        try {\n            processPartition(records.records(tp));\n            consumer.commitSync(Collections.singletonMap(tp,\n                new OffsetAndMetadata(getNextOffset(tp))));\n        } catch (Exception e) {\n            logger.error(\"Error processing partition {}\", tp, e);\n            consumer.seek(tp, consumer.position(tp));  // Retry from same offset\n        }\n    }\n} catch (WakeupException | InterruptException e) {\n    // Graceful shutdown\n    consumer.close();\n}\n```\n\n---\n\n## Configuration Properties\n\n### Critical Configuration\n\n| Property | Default | Impact |\n|----------|---------|--------|\n| `bootstrap.servers` | REQUIRED | Initial broker connections |\n| `group.id` | REQUIRED | Consumer group identifier |\n| `key.deserializer` | REQUIRED | Key deserialization class |\n| `value.deserializer` | REQUIRED | Value deserialization class |\n\n### Consumer Group Behavior\n\n| Property | Default | Purpose |\n|----------|---------|---------|\n| `max.poll.interval.ms` | 300000 | Max time between polls before expulsion |\n| `max.poll.records` | 500 | Max records per poll() |\n| `session.timeout.ms` | 45000 | Max time broker waits for heartbeat |\n| `heartbeat.interval.ms` | 3000 | Heartbeat frequency |\n\n**Recommendations:**\n\n```properties\n# For short batch processing:\nmax.poll.interval.ms=60000      # 1 minute\nmax.poll.records=100\n\n# For long-running processing:\nmax.poll.interval.ms=600000     # 10 minutes\n# Process records in parallel worker pool instead\n```\n\n### Offset Management\n\n| Property | Default | Purpose |\n|----------|---------|---------|\n| `enable.auto.commit` | true | Auto-commit offsets |\n| `auto.commit.interval.ms` | 5000 | Commit frequency |\n| `auto.offset.reset` | latest | Strategy when no offset exists |\n\n**Strategies for different semantics:**\n\n```properties\n# At-least-once:\nenable.auto.commit=true\nauto.commit.interval.ms=5000\n\n# Exactly-once:\nenable.auto.commit=false\n# Manual commit in application\n\n# Read from start:\nauto.offset.reset=earliest\n\n# Skip to end:\nauto.offset.reset=latest\n```\n\n### Network and Performance\n\n| Property | Default | Purpose |\n|----------|---------|---------|\n| `fetch.min.bytes` | 1 | Min bytes server sends |\n| `fetch.max.wait.ms` | 500 | Max time broker waits for fetch |\n| `max.partition.fetch.bytes` | 1048576 | Max bytes per partition per fetch |\n| `session.timeout.ms` | 45000 | Session timeout |\n\n### Security\n\n| Property | Purpose |\n|----------|---------|\n| `security.protocol` | SASL_SSL, SSL, SASL_PLAINTEXT |\n| `sasl.mechanism` | PLAIN, SCRAM-SHA-256, etc. |\n| `sasl.username` | Credentials |\n| `sasl.password` | Credentials |\n| `ssl.truststore.location` | Certificate store |\n\n### Isolation Level\n\n```properties\nisolation.level=read_committed  # Only read committed messages\nisolation.level=read_uncommitted  # Default, read all messages\n```\n\n**Impact on seeking:**\n\n- `read_committed`: `seekToEnd()` seeks to Last Stable Offset (LSO)\n- Records beyond LSO filtered from `poll()`\n\n---\n\n## Common Patterns and Best Practices\n\n### Pattern 1: Basic Subscription and Polling\n\n```java\nProperties props = new Properties();\nprops.put(\"bootstrap.servers\", \"localhost:9092\");\nprops.put(\"group.id\", \"my-group\");\nprops.put(\"key.deserializer\", StringDeserializer.class.getName());\nprops.put(\"value.deserializer\", StringDeserializer.class.getName());\nprops.put(\"auto.offset.reset\", \"earliest\");\n\nKafkaConsumer<String, String> consumer = new KafkaConsumer<>(props);\nconsumer.subscribe(Arrays.asList(\"topic1\", \"topic2\"));\n\ntry {\n    while (true) {\n        ConsumerRecords<String, String> records = consumer.poll(Duration.ofMillis(100));\n        for (ConsumerRecord<String, String> record : records) {\n            System.out.println(record.key() + \" -> \" + record.value());\n        }\n    }\n} finally {\n    consumer.close();\n}\n```\n\n### Pattern 2: Exactly-Once Semantics with Manual Commits\n\n```java\nProperties props = new Properties();\nprops.put(\"enable.auto.commit\", \"false\");\n\nKafkaConsumer<String, String> consumer = new KafkaConsumer<>(props);\nconsumer.subscribe(Arrays.asList(\"topic1\"));\n\ntry {\n    while (true) {\n        ConsumerRecords<String, String> records = consumer.poll(Duration.ofMillis(100));\n\n        for (TopicPartition tp : records.partitions()) {\n            List<ConsumerRecord<String, String>> partRecords = records.records(tp);\n\n            // Process all records in partition\n            for (ConsumerRecord<String, String> record : partRecords) {\n                processRecord(record);  // Must not throw exception\n            }\n\n            // Commit only after processing complete\n            ConsumerRecord<String, String> last = partRecords.get(partRecords.size() - 1);\n            consumer.commitSync(Collections.singletonMap(tp,\n                new OffsetAndMetadata(last.offset() + 1)));\n        }\n    }\n} catch (WakeupException e) {\n    logger.info(\"Shutting down\");\n} finally {\n    consumer.close();\n}\n```\n\n### Pattern 3: External Offset Storage\n\n```java\nclass ExternalOffsetStore implements ConsumerRebalanceListener {\n    private final Database db;\n    private final KafkaConsumer<String, String> consumer;\n\n    @Override\n    public void onPartitionsRevoked(Collection<TopicPartition> partitions) {\n        for (TopicPartition tp : partitions) {\n            long position = consumer.position(tp);\n            db.saveOffset(tp.topic(), tp.partition(), position);\n        }\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public void onPartitionsAssigned(Collection<TopicPartition> partitions) {\n        for (TopicPartition tp : partitions) {\n            long offset = db.loadOffset(tp.topic(), tp.partition());\n            if (offset >= 0) {\n                consumer.seek(tp, offset);\n            } else {\n                consumer.seekToBeginning(Collections.singleton(tp));\n            }\n        }\n    }\n}\n\n// Usage\nconsumer.subscribe(Arrays.asList(\"topic1\"), new ExternalOffsetStore(db, consumer));\n```\n\n### Pattern 4: Timestamp-Based Restart\n\n```java\nlong oneHourAgo = System.currentTimeMillis() - 3600_000;\n\nKafkaConsumer<String, String> consumer = new KafkaConsumer<>(props);\nconsumer.assign(Arrays.asList(\n    new TopicPartition(\"topic1\", 0),\n    new TopicPartition(\"topic1\", 1)\n));\n\nMap<TopicPartition, Long> timestampMap = new HashMap<>();\nfor (TopicPartition tp : consumer.assignment()) {\n    timestampMap.put(tp, oneHourAgo);\n}\n\nMap<TopicPartition, OffsetAndTimestamp> offsets = consumer.offsetsForTimes(timestampMap);\nfor (Map.Entry<TopicPartition, OffsetAndTimestamp> entry : offsets.entrySet()) {\n    if (entry.getValue() != null) {\n        consumer.seek(entry.getKey(), entry.getValue().offset());\n    }\n}\n```\n\n### Pattern 5: Partition-Level Pause/Resume\n\n```java\nMap<TopicPartition, Long> slowPartitionOffsets = new HashMap<>();\n\nwhile (true) {\n    ConsumerRecords<String, String> records = consumer.poll(Duration.ofMillis(100));\n\n    for (TopicPartition tp : records.partitions()) {\n        List<ConsumerRecord<String, String>> partRecords = records.records(tp);\n        long processingTime = processPartition(partRecords);\n\n        // If processing slow, pause to allow other partitions\n        if (processingTime > 1000) {\n            consumer.pause(Collections.singleton(tp));\n            slowPartitionOffsets.put(tp, partRecords.get(partRecords.size() - 1).offset() + 1);\n        }\n    }\n\n    // Resume paused partitions after delay\n    if (!slowPartitionOffsets.isEmpty()) {\n        Thread.sleep(5000);\n        consumer.resume(slowPartitionOffsets.keySet());\n    }\n}\n```\n\n### Pattern 6: Lag Monitoring\n\n```java\nScheduledExecutorService scheduler = Executors.newScheduledThreadPool(1);\n\nscheduler.scheduleAtFixedRate(() -> {\n    for (TopicPartition tp : consumer.assignment()) {\n        try {\n            long position = consumer.position(tp);\n            long end = consumer.endOffsets(Collections.singleton(tp)).get(tp);\n            long lag = end - position;\n\n            System.out.println(tp + \": lag=\" + lag);\n        } catch (Exception e) {\n            logger.error(\"Error checking lag\", e);\n        }\n    }\n}, 0, 60, TimeUnit.SECONDS);\n```\n\n### Best Practices\n\n1. **Always close consumers**: Use try-finally or try-with-resources\n2. **Handle WakeupException**: Allow graceful shutdown\n3. **Poll frequently**: Call `poll()` at least once per `max.poll.interval.ms`\n4. **Commit offset = next offset**: Committed offset should be next offset to read\n5. **Process before committing**: Commit only after successfully processing\n6. **Use callbacks for state**: Implement `ConsumerRebalanceListener` for partition-local state\n7. **Monitor lag**: Track position vs end offset to detect slowdowns\n8. **Retry transient errors**: Network timeouts are often recoverable\n9. **Test rebalancing**: Verify callbacks work correctly during group changes\n10. **Use consistent serialization**: Key and value types must match producer\n\n---\n\n## Advanced Topics\n\n### Transactional Reads\n\nWith `isolation.level=read_committed`:\n\n```properties\nisolation.level=read_committed\n```\n\n- Consumer skips records in open transactions\n- Consumer only reads up to the Last Stable Offset (LSO)\n- Ensures exactly-once semantics with transactional producer\n\n### Log Compaction Handling\n\nWith log-compacted topics:\n\n- Offsets are NOT guaranteed to be consecutive\n- Consumer may skip offsets (compacted records)\n- Use `beginningOffsets()` to find actual first offset\n- Latest value for each key always available\n\n### Consumer Lag and High-Water Mark\n\n- **High-Water Mark (HWM)**: Last offset replicated to all in-sync replicas\n- **Consumer position**: Offset of next message to fetch\n- **Consumer lag**: HWM - position\n- Lag = 0 means consumer caught up to replicated messages\n\n### Group Rebalancing Optimization\n\nFor minimal rebalance overhead:\n\n1. Set `partition.assignment.strategy=cooperative-sticky`\n2. Configure reasonable `max.poll.interval.ms`\n3. Keep `max.poll.records` moderate to avoid expulsion\n4. Use fast rebalance listeners (avoid blocking I/O)\n\n---\n\n## Summary\n\nThe Kafka `KafkaConsumer` API provides a robust, flexible mechanism for consuming messages with sophisticated offset management and group coordination. Key takeaways:\n\n- **Single-threaded**: Use one thread per consumer instance\n- **Poll-driven**: All operations happen within `poll()` calls\n- **Position tracking**: Distinguish between current position and committed offset\n- **Group coordination**: Automatic or manual partition assignment\n- **Error handling**: Different strategies for retryable vs fatal errors\n- **Offset semantics**: Committed offset = next offset to read\n- **Rebalancing**: Use listeners for proper state management\n\nProper implementation requires attention to thread safety, offset commit semantics, rebalance handling, and error recovery patterns.\n"},"caller":{"type":"direct"}}],"stop_reason":null,"stop_sequence":null,"usage":{"input_tokens":11,"cache_creation_input_tokens":2831,"cache_read_input_tokens":48235,"cache_creation":{"ephemeral_5m_input_tokens":0,"ephemeral_1h_input_tokens":2831},"output_tokens":3,"service_tier":"standard","inference_geo":"not_available"},"context_management":null},"parent_tool_use_id":null,"session_id":"48a6df13-066c-4ae9-9c41-172f077b101c","uuid":"e559a33b-5616-412b-92b4-387216aa9f07"}
